      [0;1;99m--context[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m
          The context [0;4;39mname[0m to apply for the given command.

[0;1;99mNAME[0m
      [0;1;99mstep ssh rekey[0m -- rekey a SSH certificate using the SSH CA

[0;1;99mUSAGE[0m
      [0;1;99mstep ssh rekey[0m [0;4;39mssh-cert[0m [0;4;39mssh-key[0m [[0;1;99m--out[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--issuer[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m] [[0;1;99m--password-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--force[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--offline[0m] [[0;1;99m--ca-config[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--ca-url[0m=[0;4;39muri[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--root[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--context[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m]

[0;1;99mDESCRIPTION[0m
      [0;1;99mstep ssh rekey[0m command generates a new SSH Certificate and key using
      an existing SSH Certificate and key pair to authenticate and templatize the
      request. It writes the new certificate to disk - either overwriting
      [0;4;39mssh-cert[0m or using new files when the [0;1;99m--out[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m flag is used.

[0;1;99mPOSITIONAL ARGUMENTS[0m
      [0;4;39mssh-cert[0m
          The ssh certificate to renew.

      [0;4;39mssh-key[0m
          The ssh certificate private key.

[0;1;99mOPTIONS[0m
      [0;1;99m--out[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The new key [0;4;39mfile[0m. Defaults to overwriting the [0;4;39mssh-key[0m
          positional argument.

      [0;1;99m--provisioner[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m, [0;1;99m--issuer[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m
          The provisioner [0;4;39mname[0m to use.

      [0;1;99m--provisioner-password-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The path to the [0;4;39mfile[0m containing the password to decrypt the
          one-time token generating key.

      [0;1;99m--no-password[0m
          Do not ask for a password to encrypt a private key. Sensitive key
          material will be written to disk unencrypted. This is not recommended.
          Requires [0;1;99m--insecure[0m flag.

      [0;1;99m--insecure[0m

      [0;1;99m-f[0m, [0;1;99m--force[0m
          Force the overwrite of files without asking.

      [0;1;99m--sshpop-cert[0m=[0;4;39mchain[0m
          Certificate ([0;4;39mchain[0m) in PEM format to store in the 'sshpop' header
          of a JWT.

      [0;1;99m--sshpop-key[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          Private key [0;4;39mfile[0m, used to sign a JWT, corresponding to the
          certificate that will be stored in the 'sshpop' header.

      [0;1;99m--offline[0m
          Creates a certificate without contacting the certificate authority.
          Offline mode uses the configuration, certificates, and keys created
          with [0;1;99mstep ca init[0m, but can accept a different configuration file
          using [0;1;99m--ca-config[0m flag.

      [0;1;99m--ca-config[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The certificate authority configuration [0;4;39mfile[0m. Defaults to $(step
          path)/config/ca.json

      [0;1;99m--ca-url[0m=[0;4;39mURI[0m
          [0;4;39mURI[0m of the targeted Step Certificate Authority.

      [0;1;99m--root[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The path to the PEM [0;4;39mfile[0m used as the root certificate authority.

      [0;1;99m--context[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m
          The context [0;4;39mname[0m to apply for the given command.

[0;1;99mEXAMPLES[0m
      Rekey an ssh certificate:

          $ step ssh rekey id_ecdsa-cert.pub id_ecdsa

      Rekey an ssh certificate creating id2_ecdsa, id2_ecdsa.pub, and
      id2_ecdsa-cert.pub:

          $ step ssh rekey --out id2_ecdsa id_ecdsa-cert.pub id_ecdsa

[0;1;99mNAME[0m
      [0;1;99mstep ssh renew[0m -- renew a SSH certificate using the SSH CA

[0;1;99mUSAGE[0m
      [0;1;99mstep ssh renew[0m [0;4;39mssh-cert[0m [0;4;39mssh-key[0m [[0;1;99m--out[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--issuer[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m] [[0;1;99m--password-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--force[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--offline[0m] [[0;1;99m--ca-config[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--ca-url[0m=[0;4;39muri[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--root[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--context[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m]

[0;1;99mDESCRIPTION[0m
      [0;1;99mstep ssh renew[0m command renews an SSH Host Certificate using [0;1;39mstep
      certificates[0m. It writes the new certificate to disk - either overwriting
      [0;4;39mssh-cert[0m or using a new file when the [0;1;99m--out[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m flag is used.
      This command cannot be used to renew SSH User Certificates.

[0;1;99mPOSITIONAL ARGUMENTS[0m
      [0;4;39mssh-cert[0m
          The ssh certificate to renew.

      [0;4;39mssh-key[0m
          The ssh certificate private key.

[0;1;99mOPTIONS[0m
      [0;1;99m--out[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m, [0;1;99m--output-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The new certificate [0;4;39mfile[0m. Defaults to overwriting the [0;4;39mssh-cert[0m
          positional argument

      [0;1;99m--provisioner[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m, [0;1;99m--issuer[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m
          The provisioner [0;4;39mname[0m to use.

      [0;1;99m--provisioner-password-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The path to the [0;4;39mfile[0m containing the password to decrypt the
          one-time token generating key.

      [0;1;99m--sshpop-cert[0m=[0;4;39mchain[0m
          Certificate ([0;4;39mchain[0m) in PEM format to store in the 'sshpop' header
          of a JWT.

      [0;1;99m--sshpop-key[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          Private key [0;4;39mfile[0m, used to sign a JWT, corresponding to the
          certificate that will be stored in the 'sshpop' header.

      [0;1;99m-f[0m, [0;1;99m--force[0m
          Force the overwrite of files without asking.

      [0;1;99m--offline[0m
          Creates a certificate without contacting the certificate authority.
          Offline mode uses the configuration, certificates, and keys created
          with [0;1;99mstep ca init[0m, but can accept a different configuration file
          using [0;1;99m--ca-config[0m flag.

      [0;1;99m--ca-config[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The certificate authority configuration [0;4;39mfile[0m. Defaults to $(step
          path)/config/ca.json

      [0;1;99m--ca-url[0m=[0;4;39mURI[0m
          [0;4;39mURI[0m of the targeted Step Certificate Authority.

      [0;1;99m--root[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The path to the PEM [0;4;39mfile[0m used as the root certificate authority.

      [0;1;99m--context[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m
          The context [0;4;39mname[0m to apply for the given command.

[0;1;99mEXAMPLES[0m
      Renew an ssh certificate overwriting the previous one:

          $ step ssh renew -f id_ecdsa-cert.pub id_ecdsa

      Renew an ssh certificate with a custom out file:

          $ step ssh renew -out new-id_ecdsa-cer.pub id_ecdsa-cert.pub id_ecdsa

[0;1;99mNAME[0m
      [0;1;99mstep ssh revoke[0m -- revoke a SSH certificate using the SSH CA

[0;1;99mUSAGE[0m
      [0;1;99mstep ssh revoke[0m [0;4;39mserial-number[0m [[0;1;99m--token[0m=[0;4;39mtoken[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--issuer[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m] [[0;1;99m--set[0m=[0;4;39mkey=value[0m] [[0;1;99m--set-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--password-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--reason[0m=[0;4;39mstring[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--reasonCode[0m=[0;4;39mcode[0m] [[0;1;99m--sshpop-cert[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--sshpop-key[0m=[0;4;39mkey[0m] [[0;1;99m--offline[0m] [[0;1;99m--ca-config[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--ca-url[0m=[0;4;39muri[0m] [[0;1;99m--root[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--context[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m]

[0;1;99mDESCRIPTION[0m
      [0;1;99mstep ssh revoke[0m command revokes an SSH Certificate using [0;1;39mstep
      certificates[0m.

[0;1;99mPOSITIONAL ARGUMENTS[0m
      [0;4;39mserial-number[0m
          The serial number of the SSH certificate to revoke.

[0;1;99mOPTIONS[0m
      [0;1;99m--token[0m=[0;4;39mtoken[0m
          The one-time [0;4;39mtoken[0m used to authenticate with the CA in order to
          create the certificate.

      [0;1;99m--provisioner-password-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The path to the [0;4;39mfile[0m containing the password to decrypt the
          one-time token generating key.

      [0;1;99m--provisioner[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m, [0;1;99m--issuer[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m
          The provisioner [0;4;39mname[0m to use.

      [0;1;99m--set[0m=[0;4;39mkey=value[0m
          The [0;4;39mkey=value[0m pair with template data variables. Use the [0;1;99m--set[0m
          flag multiple times to add multiple variables.

      [0;1;99m--set-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The JSON [0;4;39mfile[0m with the template data variables.

      [0;1;99m--sshpop-cert[0m=[0;4;39mchain[0m
          Certificate ([0;4;39mchain[0m) in PEM format to store in the 'sshpop' header
          of a JWT.

      [0;1;99m--sshpop-key[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          Private key [0;4;39mfile[0m, used to sign a JWT, corresponding to the
          certificate that will be stored in the 'sshpop' header.

      [0;1;99m--reason[0m=[0;4;39mstring[0m
          The [0;4;39mstring[0m representing the reason for which the cert is being
          revoked.

      [0;1;99m--reasonCode[0m=[0;4;39mreasonCode[0m
          The [0;4;39mreasonCode[0m specifies the reason for revocation - chose from a
          list of common revocation reasons. If unset, the default is
          Unspecified.

          [0;4;39mreasonCode[0m can be a number from 0-9 or a case insensitive string
          matching one of the following options:

            [0;1;99mUnspecified[0m
              No reason given (Default -- reasonCode=0).

            [0;1;99mKeyCompromise[0m
              The key is believed to have been compromised (reasonCode=1).

            [0;1;99mCACompromise[0m
              The issuing Certificate Authority itself has been compromised (reasonCode=2).

            [0;1;99mAffiliationChanged[0m
              The certificate contained affiliation information, for example, it may
              have been an EV certificate and the associated business is no longer owned by
              the same entity (reasonCode=3).

            [0;1;99mSuperseded[0m
              The certificate is being replaced (reasonCode=4).

            [0;1;99mCessationOfOperation[0m
              If a CA is decommissioned, no longer to be used, the CA's certificate
              should be revoked with this reason code. Do not revoke the CA's certificate if
              the CA no longer issues new certificates, yet still publishes CRLs for the
              currently issued certificates (reasonCode=5).

            [0;1;99mCertificateHold[0m
              A temporary revocation that indicates that a CA will not vouch for a
              certificate at a specific point in time. Once a certificate is revoked with a
              CertificateHold reason code, the certificate can then be revoked with another
              Reason Code, or unrevoked and returned to use (reasonCode=6).

            [0;1;99mRemoveFromCRL[0m
              If a certificate is revoked with the CertificateHold reason code, it is
              possible to "unrevoke" a certificate. The unrevoking process still lists the
              certificate in the CRL, but with the reason code set to RemoveFromCRL.
              Note: This is specific to the CertificateHold reason and is only used in DeltaCRLs
              (reasonCode=8).

            [0;1;99mPrivilegeWithdrawn[0m
              The right to represent the given entity was revoked for some reason
              (reasonCode=9).

            [0;1;99mAACompromise[0m
              It is known or suspected that aspects of the AA validated in the
              attribute certificate have been compromised (reasonCode=10).

      [0;1;99m--offline[0m
          Creates a certificate without contacting the certificate authority.
          Offline mode uses the configuration, certificates, and keys created
          with [0;1;99mstep ca init[0m, but can accept a different configuration file
          using [0;1;99m--ca-config[0m flag.

      [0;1;99m--ca-config[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The certificate authority configuration [0;4;39mfile[0m. Defaults to $(step
          path)/config/ca.json

      [0;1;99m--ca-url[0m=[0;4;39mURI[0m
          [0;4;39mURI[0m of the targeted Step Certificate Authority.

      [0;1;99m--root[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The path to the PEM [0;4;39mfile[0m used as the root certificate authority.

      [0;1;99m--context[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m
          The context [0;4;39mname[0m to apply for the given command.

[0;1;99mEXAMPLES[0m
      revoke an ssh certificate:

          $ step ssh revoke 3997477584487736496

[0;1;99mDESCRIPTION[0m
      [0;1;99mstep ca provisioner add[0m adds a provisioner to the CA configuration.

[0;1;99mPOSITIONAL ARGUMENTS[0m
      [0;4;39mname[0m
          The name of the provisioner.

[0;1;99mOPTIONS[0m
      [0;1;99m--type[0m=[0;4;39mtype[0m
          The [0;4;39mtype[0m of provisioner to create.

          [0;4;39mtype[0m is a case-insensitive string and must be one of:

      [0;1;99mJWK[0m
          Uses an JWK key pair to sign provisioning tokens. (default)

      [0;1;99mOIDC[0m
          Uses an OpenID Connect provider to sign provisioning tokens.

      [0;1;99mAWS[0m
          Uses Amazon AWS instance identity documents.

      [0;1;99mGCP[0m
          Use Google instance identity tokens.

      [0;1;99mAzure[0m
          Uses Microsoft Azure identity tokens.

      [0;1;99mACME[0m
          Uses the ACME protocol to create certificates.

      [0;1;99mX5C[0m
          Uses an X509 certificate / private key pair to sign provisioning
          tokens.

      [0;1;99mK8SSA[0m
          Uses Kubernetes Service Account tokens.

      [0;1;99mSSHPOP[0m
          Uses an SSH certificate / private key pair to sign provisioning
          tokens.

      [0;1;99mSCEP[0m
          Uses the SCEP protocol to create certificates.

      [0;1;99mNebula[0m
          Uses a Nebula certificate / private key pair to sign provisioning
          tokens.

      [0;1;99m--public-key[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The [0;4;39mfile[0m containing the JWK public key. Or, a [0;4;39mfile[0m containing
          one or more PEM formatted keys, if used with the K8SSA provisioner.

      [0;1;99m--create[0m
          Create the JWK key pair for the provisioner.

      [0;1;99m--private-key[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The [0;4;39mfile[0m containing the JWK private key.

      [0;1;99m--client-id[0m=[0;4;39mid[0m
          The [0;4;39mid[0m used to validate the audience in an OpenID Connect token.

      [0;1;99m--client-secret[0m=[0;4;39msecret[0m
          The [0;4;39msecret[0m used to obtain the OpenID Connect tokens.

      [0;1;99m--listen-address[0m=[0;4;39maddress[0m
          The callback [0;4;39maddress[0m used in the OpenID Connect flow (e.g.
          ":10000")

      [0;1;99m--configuration-endpoint[0m=[0;4;39murl[0m
          OpenID Connect configuration [0;4;39murl[0m.

      [0;1;99m--admin[0m=[0;4;39memail[0m
          The [0;4;39memail[0m of an admin user in an OpenID Connect provisioner, this
          user will not have restrictions in the certificates to sign. Use the
          '--admin' flag multiple times to configure multiple administrators.

      [0;1;99m--domain[0m=[0;4;39mdomain[0m
          The [0;4;39mdomain[0m used to validate the email claim in an OpenID Connect
          provisioner. Use the '--domain' flag multiple times to configure
          multiple domains.

      [0;1;99m--group[0m=[0;4;39mgroup[0m
          The [0;4;39mgroup[0m list used to validate the groups extension in an OpenID
          Connect token. Use the '--group' flag multiple times to configure
          multiple groups.

      [0;1;99m--tenant-id[0m=[0;4;39mtenant-id[0m
          The [0;4;39mtenant-id[0m used to replace the templatized tenantid value in
          the OpenID Configuration.

      [0;1;99m--x5c-roots[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m, [0;1;99m--x5c-root[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          PEM-formatted root certificate(s) [0;4;39mfile[0m used to validate the
          signature on X5C provisioning tokens.

      [0;1;99m--nebula-root[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          Root certificate (chain) [0;4;39mfile[0m used to validate the signature on
          Nebula provisioning tokens.

      [0;1;99m--require-eab[0m
          Require (and enable) External Account Binding (EAB) for Account
          creation. If this flag is set to false, then disable EAB.

      [0;1;99m--force-cn[0m
          Always set the common name in provisioned certificates.

      [0;1;99m--challenge[0m=[0;4;39mchallenge[0m
          With a SCEP provisioner the [0;4;39mchallenge[0m is a shared secret between a
          client and the CA.

      With an ACME provisioner, this flag specifies the [0;4;39mchallenge[0m or
      challenges to enable. Use the flag multiple times to configure multiple
      challenges.

      The supported ACME challenges are:

      [0;1;99mhttp-01[0m
          With the HTTP challenge, the client in an ACME transaction proves its
          control over a domain name by proving that it can provision HTTP
          resources on a server accessible under that domain name.

      [0;1;99mdns-01[0m
          With the DNS challenge, the client can prove control of a domain by
          provisioning a TXT resource record containing a designated value for a
          specific validation domain name.

      [0;1;99mtls-alpn-01[0m
          With the TLS with Application-Layer Protocol Negotiation (TLS ALPN)
          challenge, the client can prove control over a domain name by
          configuring a TLS server to respond to specific connection attempts
          using the ALPN extension with identifying information.

      [0;1;99mdevice-attest-01[0m
          With the device attestation challenge, the client can prove control
          over a permanent identifier of a device by providing an attestation
          statement containing the identifier of the device.

      If the provisioner has no challenges configured, http-01, dns-01 and
      tls-alpn-01 will be automatically enabled.

      [0;1;99m--attestation-format[0m=[0;4;39mformat[0m
          Enable an ACME attestation statement [0;4;39mformat[0m in the provisioner.
          Use the flag multiple times to configure multiple challenges.

      The supported ACME attestation formats are:

      [0;1;99mapple[0m
          With the apple format, Apple devices can use the device-attest-01
          challenge to get a new certificate.

      [0;1;99mstep[0m
          With the step format, devices like YubiKeys that can generate an
          attestation certificate can use the device-attest-01 challenge to get a
          new certificate.

      [0;1;99mtpm[0m
          With the tpm format, devices with TPMs can use the device-attest-01
          challenge to get a new certificate.

      [0;1;99m--attestation-roots[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          PEM-formatted root certificate(s) [0;4;39mfile[0m used to validate the
          attestation certificates. Use the flag multiple times to read from
          multiple files.

      [0;1;99m--capabilities[0m=[0;4;39mcapabilities[0m
          The SCEP [0;4;39mcapabilities[0m to advertise

      [0;1;99m--include-root[0m
          Include the CA root certificate in the SCEP CA certificate chain

      [0;1;99m--exclude-intermediate[0m
          Exclude the CA intermediate certificate in the SCEP CA certificate
          chain

      [0;1;99m--min-public-key-length[0m=[0;4;39mlength[0m
          The minimum public key [0;4;39mlength[0m of the SCEP RSA encryption key

      [0;1;99m--encryption-algorithm-identifier[0m=[0;4;39mid[0m
          The [0;4;39mid[0m for the SCEP encryption algorithm to use. Valid values are
          0 - 4, inclusive. The values correspond to: 0: DES-CBC, 1: AES-128-CBC,
          2: AES-256-CBC, 3: AES-128-GCM, 4: AES-256-GCM. Defaults to DES-CBC (0)
          for legacy clients.

      [0;1;99m--scep-decrypter-certificate-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The path to a PEM certificate [0;4;39mfile[0m for the SCEP decrypter

      [0;1;99m--scep-decrypter-key-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The path to a PEM private key [0;4;39mfile[0m for the SCEP decrypter

      [0;1;99m--scep-decrypter-key-uri[0m=[0;4;39muri[0m
          The key [0;4;39muri[0m for the SCEP decrypter. Should be a valid value for
          the KMS type used.

      [0;1;99m--scep-decrypter-key-password-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The path to a [0;4;39mfile[0m containing the password for the SCEP decrypter
          key

      [0;1;99m--aws-account[0m=[0;4;39mid[0m
          The AWS account [0;4;39mid[0m used to validate the identity documents. Use
          the flag multiple times to configure multiple accounts.

      [0;1;99m--azure-tenant[0m=[0;4;39mid[0m
          The Microsoft Azure tenant [0;4;39mid[0m used to validate the identity
          tokens.

      [0;1;99m--azure-resource-group[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m
          The Microsoft Azure resource group [0;4;39mname[0m used to validate the
          identity tokens. Use the flag multiple times to configure multiple
          resource groups

      [0;1;99m--azure-audience[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m
          The Microsoft Azure audience [0;4;39mname[0m used to validate the identity
          tokens.

      [0;1;99m--azure-subscription-id[0m=[0;4;39mid[0m
          The Microsoft Azure subscription [0;4;39mid[0m used to validate the identity
          tokens. Use the flag multiple times to configure multiple subscription
          IDs

      [0;1;99m--azure-object-id[0m=[0;4;39mid[0m
          The Microsoft Azure AD object [0;4;39mid[0m used to validate the identity
          tokens. Use the flag multiple times to configure multiple object IDs

      [0;1;99m--gcp-service-account[0m=[0;4;39memail[0m
          The Google service account [0;4;39memail[0m or [0;4;39mid[0m used to validate the
          identity tokens. Use the flag multiple times to configure multiple
          service accounts.

      [0;1;99m--gcp-project[0m=[0;4;39mid[0m
          The Google project [0;4;39mid[0m used to validate the identity tokens. Use
          the flag multiple times to configure multiple projects

      [0;1;99m--gcp-organization[0m=[0;4;39mid[0m
          The Google organization [0;4;39mid[0m used to validate the project in the
          identity tokens.

      [0;1;99m--instance-age[0m=[0;4;39mduration[0m
          The maximum [0;4;39mduration[0m to grant a certificate in AWS and GCP
          provisioners. A [0;4;39mduration[0m is sequence of decimal numbers, each with
          optional fraction and a unit suffix, such as "300ms", "-1.5h" or
          "2h45m". Valid time units are "ns", "us" (or "µs"), "ms", "s", "m",
          "h".

      [0;1;99m--disable-custom-sans[0m
          On cloud provisioners, if enabled only the internal DNS and IP will be
          added as a SAN. By default it will accept any SAN in the CSR.

      [0;1;99m--disable-trust-on-first-use[0m, [0;1;99m--disable-tofu[0m
          On cloud provisioners, if enabled multiple sign request for this
          provisioner with the same instance will be accepted. By default only
          the first request will be accepted.

      [0;1;99m--disable-ssh-ca-user[0m
          Disable ability to sign SSH user certificates

      [0;1;99m--disable-ssh-ca-host[0m
          Disable ability to sign SSH host certificates

      [0;1;99m--x509-template[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The x509 certificate template [0;4;39mfile[0m, a JSON representation of the
          certificate to create.

      [0;1;99m--x509-template-data[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The x509 certificate template data [0;4;39mfile[0m, a JSON map of data that
          can be used by the certificate template.

      [0;1;99m--ssh-template[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The x509 certificate template [0;4;39mfile[0m, a JSON representation of the
          certificate to create.

      [0;1;99m--ssh-template-data[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The ssh certificate template data [0;4;39mfile[0m, a JSON map of data that
          can be used by the certificate template.

      [0;1;99m--x509-min-dur[0m=[0;4;39mduration[0m
          The minimum [0;4;39mduration[0m for an x509 certificate generated by this
          provisioner. Value must be a sequence of decimal numbers, each with
          optional fraction, and a unit suffix, such as "300ms", "-1.5h" or
          "2h45m". Valid time units are "ns", "us" (or "µs"), "ms", "s", "m",
          "h".

      [0;1;99m--x509-max-dur[0m=[0;4;39mduration[0m
          The maximum [0;4;39mduration[0m for an x509 certificate generated by this
          provisioner. Value must be a sequence of decimal numbers, each with
          optional fraction, and a unit suffix, such as "300ms", "-1.5h" or
          "2h45m". Valid time units are "ns", "us" (or "µs"), "ms", "s", "m",
          "h".

      [0;1;99m--x509-default-dur[0m=[0;4;39mduration[0m
          The default [0;4;39mduration[0m for an x509 certificate generated by this
          provisioner. Value must be a sequence of decimal numbers, each with
          optional fraction, and a unit suffix, such as "300ms", "-1.5h" or
          "2h45m". Valid time units are "ns", "us" (or "µs"), "ms", "s", "m",
          "h".

      [0;1;99m--ssh-user-min-dur[0m=[0;4;39mduration[0m
          The minimum [0;4;39mduration[0m for an ssh user certificate generated by this
          provisioner. Value must be a sequence of decimal numbers, each with
          optional fraction, and a unit suffix, such as "300ms", "-1.5h" or
          "2h45m". Valid time units are "ns", "us" (or "µs"), "ms", "s", "m",
          "h".

      [0;1;99m--ssh-user-max-dur[0m=[0;4;39mduration[0m
          The maximum [0;4;39mduration[0m for an ssh user certificate generated by this
          provisioner. Value must be a sequence of decimal numbers, each with
          optional fraction, and a unit suffix, such as "300ms", "-1.5h" or
          "2h45m". Valid time units are "ns", "us" (or "µs"), "ms", "s", "m",
          "h".

      [0;1;99m--ssh-user-default-dur[0m=[0;4;39mduration[0m
          The maximum [0;4;39mduration[0m for an ssh user certificate generated by this
          provisioner. Value must be a sequence of decimal numbers, each with
          optional fraction, and a unit suffix, such as "300ms", "-1.5h" or
          "2h45m". Valid time units are "ns", "us" (or "µs"), "ms", "s", "m",
          "h".

      [0;1;99m--ssh-host-min-dur[0m=[0;4;39mduration[0m
          The minimum [0;4;39mduration[0m for an ssh host certificate generated by this
          provisioner. Value must be a sequence of decimal numbers, each with
          optional fraction, and a unit suffix, such as "300ms", "-1.5h" or
          "2h45m". Valid time units are "ns", "us" (or "µs"), "ms", "s", "m",
          "h".

      [0;1;99m--ssh-host-max-dur[0m=[0;4;39mduration[0m
          The maximum [0;4;39mduration[0m for an ssh host certificate generated by this
          provisioner. Value must be a sequence of decimal numbers, each with
          optional fraction, and a unit suffix, such as "300ms", "-1.5h" or
          "2h45m". Valid time units are "ns", "us" (or "µs"), "ms", "s", "m",
          "h".

      [0;1;99m--ssh-host-default-dur[0m=[0;4;39mduration[0m
          The maximum [0;4;39mduration[0m for an ssh host certificate generated by this
          provisioner. Value must be a sequence of decimal numbers, each with
          optional fraction, and a unit suffix, such as "300ms", "-1.5h" or
          "2h45m". Valid time units are "ns", "us" (or "µs"), "ms", "s", "m",
          "h".

      [0;1;99m--disable-renewal[0m
          Disable renewal for all certificates generated by this provisioner.

      [0;1;99m--allow-renewal-after-expiry[0m
          Allow renewals for expired certificates generated by this provisioner.

      [0;1;99m--disable-smallstep-extensions[0m
          Disable the Smallstep extension for all certificates generated by this
          provisioner.

      [0;1;99m--ssh[0m
          Enable provisioning of ssh certificates. The default value is true. To
          disable ssh use '--ssh=false'.

      [0;1;99m--admin-cert[0m=[0;4;39mchain[0m
          Admin certificate ([0;4;39mchain[0m) in PEM format to store in the 'x5c'
          header of a JWT.

      [0;1;99m--admin-key[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          Private key [0;4;39mfile[0m, used to sign a JWT, corresponding to the admin
          certificate that will be stored in the 'x5c' header.

      [0;1;99m--admin-subject[0m=[0;4;39msubject[0m, [0;1;99m--admin-name[0m=[0;4;39msubject[0m
          The admin [0;4;39msubject[0m to use for generating admin credentials.

      [0;1;99m--admin-provisioner[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m, [0;1;99m--admin-issuer[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m
          The provisioner [0;4;39mname[0m to use for generating admin credentials.

      [0;1;99m--admin-password-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The path to the [0;4;39mfile[0m containing the password to decrypt the
          one-time token generating key.

      [0;1;99m--password-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The path to the [0;4;39mfile[0m containing the password to encrypt or decrypt
          the private key.

      [0;1;99m--ca-url[0m=[0;4;39mURI[0m
          [0;4;39mURI[0m of the targeted Step Certificate Authority.

      [0;1;99m--root[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The path to the PEM [0;4;39mfile[0m used as the root certificate authority.

      [0;1;99m--context[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m
          The context [0;4;39mname[0m to apply for the given command.

      [0;1;99m--ca-config[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The certificate authority configuration [0;4;39mfile[0m. Defaults to $(step
          path)/config/ca.json

[0;1;99mEXAMPLES[0m
      Create a JWK provisioner with newly generated keys and a template for x509
      certificates:

          step ca provisioner add cicd --type JWK --create --x509-template ./templates/example.tpl

      Create a JWK provisioner and explicitly select the configuration file to
      update:

          step ca provisioner add cicd --type JWK --create --ca-config /path/to/ca.json

      Create a JWK provisioner with duration claims:

          step ca provisioner add cicd --type JWK --create --x509-min-dur 20m --x509-default-dur 48h --ssh-user-min-dur 17m --ssh-host-default-dur 16h

      Create a JWK provisioner with existing keys:

          step ca provisioner add jane@doe.com --type JWK --public-key jwk.pub --private-key jwk.priv

      Create an OIDC provisioner:

          step ca provisioner add Google --type OIDC --ssh \
            --client-id 1087160488420-8qt7bavg3qesdhs6it824mhnfgcfe8il.apps.googleusercontent.com \
            --client-secret udTrOT3gzrO7W9fDPgZQLfYJ \
            --configuration-endpoint https://accounts.google.com/.well-known/openid-configuration

      Create an X5C provisioner:

          step ca provisioner add x5c --type X5C --x5c-roots x5c_ca.crt

      Create an ACME provisioner:

          step ca provisioner add acme --type ACME

      Create an ACME provisioner, forcing a CN and requiring EAB:

          step ca provisioner add acme --type ACME --force-cn --require-eab

      Create an ACME provisioner for device attestation:

          step ca provisioner add attestation --type ACME --challenge device-attest-01

      Create an K8SSA provisioner:

          step ca provisioner add kube --type K8SSA --ssh --public-key key.pub

      Create an SSHPOP provisioner for renewing SSH host certificates:")

          step ca provisioner add sshpop --type SSHPOP

      Create a SCEP provisioner with 'secret' challenge and AES-256-CBC
      encryption:

          step ca provisioner add my_scep_provisioner --type SCEP --challenge secret --encryption-algorithm-identifier 2

      Create an Azure provisioner with two resource groups, one subscription ID
      and one object ID:

          $ step ca provisioner add Azure --type Azure \
            --azure-tenant bc9043e2-b645-4c1c-a87a-78f8644bfe57 \
            --azure-resource-group identity --azure-resource-group accounting \
            --azure-subscription-id dc760a01-2886-4a84-9abc-f3508e0f87d9 \
            --azure-object-id f50926c7-abbf-4c28-87dc-9adc7eaf3ba7

      Create a GCP provisioner that will only accept the SANs provided in the
      identity token:

          $ step ca provisioner add Google --type GCP \
            --disable-custom-sans --gcp-project internal

      Create a GCP provisioner that can be used across all projects within an
      organization:

          $ step ca provisioner add Google --type GCP --gcp-organization 123456789

      Create an AWS provisioner that will only accept the SANs provided in the
      identity document and will allow multiple certificates from the same
      instance:

          $ step ca provisioner add Amazon --type AWS \
            --aws-account 123456789 --disable-custom-sans --disable-trust-on-first-use

      Create an AWS provisioner that will use a custom certificate to validate
      the instance identity documents:

          $ step ca provisioner add Amazon --type AWS \
            --aws-account 123456789

[0;1;99mNAME[0m
      [0;1;99mstep ca provisioner add[0m -- add a provisioner

[0;1;99mUSAGE[0m
      [0;1;99mstep ca provisioner add[0m [0;4;39mname[0m [0;1;99m--type[0m=JWK
      [[0;1;99m--public-key[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--private-key[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--create[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--password-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--admin-cert[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--admin-key[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--admin-subject[0m=[0;4;39msubject[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--admin-provisioner[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m] [[0;1;99m--admin-password-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--ca-url[0m=[0;4;39muri[0m] [[0;1;99m--root[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--context[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--ca-config[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--x509-template[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--x509-template-data[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--ssh-template[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--ssh-template-data[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m]

      ACME

      [0;1;99mstep ca provisioner add[0m [0;4;39mname[0m [0;1;99m--type[0m=ACME [[0;1;99m--force-cn[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--require-eab[0m] [[0;1;99m--challenge[0m=[0;4;39mchallenge[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--attestation-format[0m=[0;4;39mformat[0m] [[0;1;99m--attestation-roots[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--admin-cert[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--admin-key[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--admin-subject[0m=[0;4;39msubject[0m] [[0;1;99m--admin-provisioner[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--admin-password-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--ca-url[0m=[0;4;39muri[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--root[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--context[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m] [[0;1;99m--ca-config[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--x509-template[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--x509-template-data[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m]

      OIDC

      [0;1;99mstep ca provisioner add[0m [0;4;39mname[0m [0;1;99m--type[0m=OIDC
      [[0;1;99m--client-id[0m=[0;4;39mid[0m] [[0;1;99m--client-secret[0m=[0;4;39msecret[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--configuration-endpoint[0m=[0;4;39murl[0m] [[0;1;99m--domain[0m=[0;4;39mdomain[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--admin[0m=[0;4;39memail[0m]... [[0;1;99m--admin-cert[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--admin-key[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--admin-subject[0m=[0;4;39msubject[0m]

      SCEP

      [0;1;99mstep ca provisioner add[0m [0;4;39mname[0m [0;1;99m--type[0m=SCEP [[0;1;99m--force-cn[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--challenge[0m=[0;4;39mchallenge[0m] [[0;1;99m--capabilities[0m=[0;4;39mcapabilities[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--include-root[0m] [[0;1;99m--exclude-intermediate[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--min-public-key-length[0m=[0;4;39mlength[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--encryption-algorithm-identifier[0m=[0;4;39mid[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--scep-decrypter-certificate-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--scep-decrypter-key-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--scep-decrypter-key-uri[0m=[0;4;39muri[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--scep-decrypter-key-password-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--admin-cert[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--admin-key[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--admin-subject[0m=[0;4;39msubject[0m]

      [[0;1;99m--ca-url[0m=[0;4;39muri[0m] [[0;1;99m--root[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--context[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--ca-config[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m] [[0;1;99m--x509-template[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m]
      [[0;1;99m--x509-template-data[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m]

[0;1;99mDESCRIPTION[0m
      [0;1;99mstep ca provisioner add[0m adds a provisioner to the CA configuration.

[0;1;99mPOSITIONAL ARGUMENTS[0m
      [0;4;39mname[0m
          The name of the provisioner.

[0;1;99mOPTIONS[0m
      [0;1;99m--type[0m=[0;4;39mtype[0m
          The [0;4;39mtype[0m of provisioner to create.

          [0;4;39mtype[0m is a case-insensitive string and must be one of:

      [0;1;99mJWK[0m
          Uses an JWK key pair to sign provisioning tokens. (default)

      [0;1;99mOIDC[0m
          Uses an OpenID Connect provider to sign provisioning tokens.

      [0;1;99mAWS[0m
          Uses Amazon AWS instance identity documents.

      [0;1;99mGCP[0m
          Use Google instance identity tokens.

      [0;1;99mAzure[0m
          Uses Microsoft Azure identity tokens.

      [0;1;99mACME[0m
          Uses the ACME protocol to create certificates.

      [0;1;99mX5C[0m
          Uses an X509 certificate / private key pair to sign provisioning
          tokens.

      [0;1;99mK8SSA[0m
          Uses Kubernetes Service Account tokens.

      [0;1;99mSSHPOP[0m
          Uses an SSH certificate / private key pair to sign provisioning
          tokens.

      [0;1;99mSCEP[0m
          Uses the SCEP protocol to create certificates.

      [0;1;99mNebula[0m
          Uses a Nebula certificate / private key pair to sign provisioning
          tokens.

      [0;1;99m--public-key[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The [0;4;39mfile[0m containing the JWK public key. Or, a [0;4;39mfile[0m containing
          one or more PEM formatted keys, if used with the K8SSA provisioner.

      [0;1;99m--create[0m
          Create the JWK key pair for the provisioner.

      [0;1;99m--private-key[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The [0;4;39mfile[0m containing the JWK private key.

      [0;1;99m--client-id[0m=[0;4;39mid[0m
          The [0;4;39mid[0m used to validate the audience in an OpenID Connect token.

      [0;1;99m--client-secret[0m=[0;4;39msecret[0m
          The [0;4;39msecret[0m used to obtain the OpenID Connect tokens.

      [0;1;99m--listen-address[0m=[0;4;39maddress[0m
          The callback [0;4;39maddress[0m used in the OpenID Connect flow (e.g.
          ":10000")

      [0;1;99m--configuration-endpoint[0m=[0;4;39murl[0m
          OpenID Connect configuration [0;4;39murl[0m.

      [0;1;99m--admin[0m=[0;4;39memail[0m
          The [0;4;39memail[0m of an admin user in an OpenID Connect provisioner, this
          user will not have restrictions in the certificates to sign. Use the
          '--admin' flag multiple times to configure multiple administrators.

      [0;1;99m--domain[0m=[0;4;39mdomain[0m
          The [0;4;39mdomain[0m used to validate the email claim in an OpenID Connect
          provisioner. Use the '--domain' flag multiple times to configure
          multiple domains.

      [0;1;99m--group[0m=[0;4;39mgroup[0m
          The [0;4;39mgroup[0m list used to validate the groups extension in an OpenID
          Connect token. Use the '--group' flag multiple times to configure
          multiple groups.

      [0;1;99m--tenant-id[0m=[0;4;39mtenant-id[0m
          The [0;4;39mtenant-id[0m used to replace the templatized tenantid value in
          the OpenID Configuration.

      [0;1;99m--x5c-roots[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m, [0;1;99m--x5c-root[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          PEM-formatted root certificate(s) [0;4;39mfile[0m used to validate the
          signature on X5C provisioning tokens.

      [0;1;99m--nebula-root[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          Root certificate (chain) [0;4;39mfile[0m used to validate the signature on
          Nebula provisioning tokens.

      [0;1;99m--require-eab[0m
          Require (and enable) External Account Binding (EAB) for Account
          creation. If this flag is set to false, then disable EAB.

      [0;1;99m--force-cn[0m
          Always set the common name in provisioned certificates.

      [0;1;99m--challenge[0m=[0;4;39mchallenge[0m
          With a SCEP provisioner the [0;4;39mchallenge[0m is a shared secret between a
          client and the CA.

      With an ACME provisioner, this flag specifies the [0;4;39mchallenge[0m or
      challenges to enable. Use the flag multiple times to configure multiple
      challenges.

      The supported ACME challenges are:

      [0;1;99mhttp-01[0m
          With the HTTP challenge, the client in an ACME transaction proves its
          control over a domain name by proving that it can provision HTTP
          resources on a server accessible under that domain name.

      [0;1;99mdns-01[0m
          With the DNS challenge, the client can prove control of a domain by
          provisioning a TXT resource record containing a designated value for a
          specific validation domain name.

      [0;1;99mtls-alpn-01[0m
          With the TLS with Application-Layer Protocol Negotiation (TLS ALPN)
          challenge, the client can prove control over a domain name by
          configuring a TLS server to respond to specific connection attempts
          using the ALPN extension with identifying information.

      [0;1;99mdevice-attest-01[0m
          With the device attestation challenge, the client can prove control
          over a permanent identifier of a device by providing an attestation
          statement containing the identifier of the device.

      If the provisioner has no challenges configured, http-01, dns-01 and
      tls-alpn-01 will be automatically enabled.

      [0;1;99m--attestation-format[0m=[0;4;39mformat[0m
          Enable an ACME attestation statement [0;4;39mformat[0m in the provisioner.
          Use the flag multiple times to configure multiple challenges.

      The supported ACME attestation formats are:

      [0;1;99mapple[0m
          With the apple format, Apple devices can use the device-attest-01
          challenge to get a new certificate.

      [0;1;99mstep[0m
          With the step format, devices like YubiKeys that can generate an
          attestation certificate can use the device-attest-01 challenge to get a
          new certificate.

      [0;1;99mtpm[0m
          With the tpm format, devices with TPMs can use the device-attest-01
          challenge to get a new certificate.

      [0;1;99m--attestation-roots[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          PEM-formatted root certificate(s) [0;4;39mfile[0m used to validate the
          attestation certificates. Use the flag multiple times to read from
          multiple files.

      [0;1;99m--capabilities[0m=[0;4;39mcapabilities[0m
          The SCEP [0;4;39mcapabilities[0m to advertise

      [0;1;99m--include-root[0m
          Include the CA root certificate in the SCEP CA certificate chain

      [0;1;99m--exclude-intermediate[0m
          Exclude the CA intermediate certificate in the SCEP CA certificate
          chain

      [0;1;99m--min-public-key-length[0m=[0;4;39mlength[0m
          The minimum public key [0;4;39mlength[0m of the SCEP RSA encryption key

      [0;1;99m--encryption-algorithm-identifier[0m=[0;4;39mid[0m
          The [0;4;39mid[0m for the SCEP encryption algorithm to use. Valid values are
          0 - 4, inclusive. The values correspond to: 0: DES-CBC, 1: AES-128-CBC,
          2: AES-256-CBC, 3: AES-128-GCM, 4: AES-256-GCM. Defaults to DES-CBC (0)
          for legacy clients.

      [0;1;99m--scep-decrypter-certificate-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The path to a PEM certificate [0;4;39mfile[0m for the SCEP decrypter

      [0;1;99m--scep-decrypter-key-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The path to a PEM private key [0;4;39mfile[0m for the SCEP decrypter

      [0;1;99m--scep-decrypter-key-uri[0m=[0;4;39muri[0m
          The key [0;4;39muri[0m for the SCEP decrypter. Should be a valid value for
          the KMS type used.

      [0;1;99m--scep-decrypter-key-password-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The path to a [0;4;39mfile[0m containing the password for the SCEP decrypter
          key

      [0;1;99m--aws-account[0m=[0;4;39mid[0m
          The AWS account [0;4;39mid[0m used to validate the identity documents. Use
          the flag multiple times to configure multiple accounts.

      [0;1;99m--azure-tenant[0m=[0;4;39mid[0m
          The Microsoft Azure tenant [0;4;39mid[0m used to validate the identity
          tokens.

      [0;1;99m--azure-resource-group[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m
          The Microsoft Azure resource group [0;4;39mname[0m used to validate the
          identity tokens. Use the flag multiple times to configure multiple
          resource groups

      [0;1;99m--azure-audience[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m
          The Microsoft Azure audience [0;4;39mname[0m used to validate the identity
          tokens.

      [0;1;99m--azure-subscription-id[0m=[0;4;39mid[0m
          The Microsoft Azure subscription [0;4;39mid[0m used to validate the identity
          tokens. Use the flag multiple times to configure multiple subscription
          IDs

      [0;1;99m--azure-object-id[0m=[0;4;39mid[0m
          The Microsoft Azure AD object [0;4;39mid[0m used to validate the identity
          tokens. Use the flag multiple times to configure multiple object IDs

      [0;1;99m--gcp-service-account[0m=[0;4;39memail[0m
          The Google service account [0;4;39memail[0m or [0;4;39mid[0m used to validate the
          identity tokens. Use the flag multiple times to configure multiple
          service accounts.

      [0;1;99m--gcp-project[0m=[0;4;39mid[0m
          The Google project [0;4;39mid[0m used to validate the identity tokens. Use
          the flag multiple times to configure multiple projects

      [0;1;99m--gcp-organization[0m=[0;4;39mid[0m
          The Google organization [0;4;39mid[0m used to validate the project in the
          identity tokens.

      [0;1;99m--instance-age[0m=[0;4;39mduration[0m
          The maximum [0;4;39mduration[0m to grant a certificate in AWS and GCP
          provisioners. A [0;4;39mduration[0m is sequence of decimal numbers, each with
          optional fraction and a unit suffix, such as "300ms", "-1.5h" or
          "2h45m". Valid time units are "ns", "us" (or "µs"), "ms", "s", "m",
          "h".

      [0;1;99m--disable-custom-sans[0m
          On cloud provisioners, if enabled only the internal DNS and IP will be
          added as a SAN. By default it will accept any SAN in the CSR.

      [0;1;99m--disable-trust-on-first-use[0m, [0;1;99m--disable-tofu[0m
          On cloud provisioners, if enabled multiple sign request for this
          provisioner with the same instance will be accepted. By default only
          the first request will be accepted.

      [0;1;99m--disable-ssh-ca-user[0m
          Disable ability to sign SSH user certificates

      [0;1;99m--disable-ssh-ca-host[0m
          Disable ability to sign SSH host certificates

      [0;1;99m--x509-template[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The x509 certificate template [0;4;39mfile[0m, a JSON representation of the
          certificate to create.

      [0;1;99m--x509-template-data[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The x509 certificate template data [0;4;39mfile[0m, a JSON map of data that
          can be used by the certificate template.

      [0;1;99m--ssh-template[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The x509 certificate template [0;4;39mfile[0m, a JSON representation of the
          certificate to create.

      [0;1;99m--ssh-template-data[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The ssh certificate template data [0;4;39mfile[0m, a JSON map of data that
          can be used by the certificate template.

      [0;1;99m--x509-min-dur[0m=[0;4;39mduration[0m
          The minimum [0;4;39mduration[0m for an x509 certificate generated by this
          provisioner. Value must be a sequence of decimal numbers, each with
          optional fraction, and a unit suffix, such as "300ms", "-1.5h" or
          "2h45m". Valid time units are "ns", "us" (or "µs"), "ms", "s", "m",
          "h".

      [0;1;99m--x509-max-dur[0m=[0;4;39mduration[0m
          The maximum [0;4;39mduration[0m for an x509 certificate generated by this
          provisioner. Value must be a sequence of decimal numbers, each with
          optional fraction, and a unit suffix, such as "300ms", "-1.5h" or
          "2h45m". Valid time units are "ns", "us" (or "µs"), "ms", "s", "m",
          "h".

      [0;1;99m--x509-default-dur[0m=[0;4;39mduration[0m
          The default [0;4;39mduration[0m for an x509 certificate generated by this
          provisioner. Value must be a sequence of decimal numbers, each with
          optional fraction, and a unit suffix, such as "300ms", "-1.5h" or
          "2h45m". Valid time units are "ns", "us" (or "µs"), "ms", "s", "m",
          "h".

      [0;1;99m--ssh-user-min-dur[0m=[0;4;39mduration[0m
          The minimum [0;4;39mduration[0m for an ssh user certificate generated by this
          provisioner. Value must be a sequence of decimal numbers, each with
          optional fraction, and a unit suffix, such as "300ms", "-1.5h" or
          "2h45m". Valid time units are "ns", "us" (or "µs"), "ms", "s", "m",
          "h".

      [0;1;99m--ssh-user-max-dur[0m=[0;4;39mduration[0m
          The maximum [0;4;39mduration[0m for an ssh user certificate generated by this
          provisioner. Value must be a sequence of decimal numbers, each with
          optional fraction, and a unit suffix, such as "300ms", "-1.5h" or
          "2h45m". Valid time units are "ns", "us" (or "µs"), "ms", "s", "m",
          "h".

      [0;1;99m--ssh-user-default-dur[0m=[0;4;39mduration[0m
          The maximum [0;4;39mduration[0m for an ssh user certificate generated by this
          provisioner. Value must be a sequence of decimal numbers, each with
          optional fraction, and a unit suffix, such as "300ms", "-1.5h" or
          "2h45m". Valid time units are "ns", "us" (or "µs"), "ms", "s", "m",
          "h".

      [0;1;99m--ssh-host-min-dur[0m=[0;4;39mduration[0m
          The minimum [0;4;39mduration[0m for an ssh host certificate generated by this
          provisioner. Value must be a sequence of decimal numbers, each with
          optional fraction, and a unit suffix, such as "300ms", "-1.5h" or
          "2h45m". Valid time units are "ns", "us" (or "µs"), "ms", "s", "m",
          "h".

      [0;1;99m--ssh-host-max-dur[0m=[0;4;39mduration[0m
          The maximum [0;4;39mduration[0m for an ssh host certificate generated by this
          provisioner. Value must be a sequence of decimal numbers, each with
          optional fraction, and a unit suffix, such as "300ms", "-1.5h" or
          "2h45m". Valid time units are "ns", "us" (or "µs"), "ms", "s", "m",
          "h".

      [0;1;99m--ssh-host-default-dur[0m=[0;4;39mduration[0m
          The maximum [0;4;39mduration[0m for an ssh host certificate generated by this
          provisioner. Value must be a sequence of decimal numbers, each with
          optional fraction, and a unit suffix, such as "300ms", "-1.5h" or
          "2h45m". Valid time units are "ns", "us" (or "µs"), "ms", "s", "m",
          "h".

      [0;1;99m--disable-renewal[0m
          Disable renewal for all certificates generated by this provisioner.

      [0;1;99m--allow-renewal-after-expiry[0m
          Allow renewals for expired certificates generated by this provisioner.

      [0;1;99m--disable-smallstep-extensions[0m
          Disable the Smallstep extension for all certificates generated by this
          provisioner.

      [0;1;99m--ssh[0m
          Enable provisioning of ssh certificates. The default value is true. To
          disable ssh use '--ssh=false'.

      [0;1;99m--admin-cert[0m=[0;4;39mchain[0m
          Admin certificate ([0;4;39mchain[0m) in PEM format to store in the 'x5c'
          header of a JWT.

      [0;1;99m--admin-key[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          Private key [0;4;39mfile[0m, used to sign a JWT, corresponding to the admin
          certificate that will be stored in the 'x5c' header.

      [0;1;99m--admin-subject[0m=[0;4;39msubject[0m, [0;1;99m--admin-name[0m=[0;4;39msubject[0m
          The admin [0;4;39msubject[0m to use for generating admin credentials.

      [0;1;99m--admin-provisioner[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m, [0;1;99m--admin-issuer[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m
          The provisioner [0;4;39mname[0m to use for generating admin credentials.

      [0;1;99m--admin-password-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The path to the [0;4;39mfile[0m containing the password to decrypt the
          one-time token generating key.

      [0;1;99m--password-file[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The path to the [0;4;39mfile[0m containing the password to encrypt or decrypt
          the private key.

      [0;1;99m--ca-url[0m=[0;4;39mURI[0m
          [0;4;39mURI[0m of the targeted Step Certificate Authority.

      [0;1;99m--root[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The path to the PEM [0;4;39mfile[0m used as the root certificate authority.

      [0;1;99m--context[0m=[0;4;39mname[0m
          The context [0;4;39mname[0m to apply for the given command.

      [0;1;99m--ca-config[0m=[0;4;39mfile[0m
          The certificate authority configuration [0;4;39mfile[0m. Defaults to $(step
          path)/config/ca.json

[0;1;99mEXAMPLES[0m
      Create a JWK provisioner with newly generated keys and a template for x509
      certificates:

          step ca provisioner add cicd --type JWK --create --x509-template ./templates/example.tpl

      Create a JWK provisioner and explicitly select the configuration file to
      update:

          step ca provisioner add cicd --type JWK --create --ca-config /path/to/ca.json

      Create a JWK provisioner with duration claims:

          step ca provisioner add cicd --type JWK --create --x509-min-dur 20m --x509-default-dur 48h --ssh-user-min-dur 17m --ssh-host-default-dur 16h

      Create a JWK provisioner with existing keys:

          step ca provisioner add jane@doe.com --type JWK --public-key jwk.pub --private-key jwk.priv

      Create an OIDC provisioner:

          step ca provisioner add Google --type OIDC --ssh \
            --client-id 1087160488420-8qt7bavg3qesdhs6it824mhnfgcfe8il.apps.googleusercontent.com \
            --client-secret udTrOT3gzrO7W9fDPgZQLfYJ \
            --configuration-endpoint https://accounts.google.com/.well-known/openid-configuration

      Create an X5C provisioner:

          step ca provisioner add x5c --type X5C --x5c-roots x5c_ca.crt

      Create an ACME provisioner:

          step ca provisioner add acme --type ACME

      Create an ACME provisioner, forcing a CN and requiring EAB:

          step ca provisioner add acme --type ACME --force-cn --require-eab

      Create an ACME provisioner for device attestation:

          step ca provisioner add attestation --type ACME --challenge device-attest-01

      Create an K8SSA provisioner:

          step ca provisioner add kube --type K8SSA --ssh --public-key key.pub

      Create an SSHPOP provisioner for renewing SSH host certificates:")

          step ca provisioner add sshpop --type SSHPOP

      Create a SCEP provisioner with 'secret' challenge and AES-256-CBC
      encryption:

          step ca provisioner add my_scep_provisioner --type SCEP --challenge secret --encryption-algorithm-identifier 2

      Create an Azure provisioner with two resource groups, one subscription ID
      and one object ID:

          $ step ca provisioner add Azure --type Azure \
            --azure-tenant bc9043e2-b645-4c1c-a87a-78f8644bfe57 \
            --azure-resource-group identity --azure-resource-group accounting \
            --azure-subscription-id dc760a01-2886-4a84-9abc-f3508e0f87d9 \
            --azure-object-id f50926c7-abbf-4c28-87dc-9adc7eaf3ba7

      Create a GCP provisioner that will only accept the SANs provided in the
      identity token:

          $ step ca provisioner add Google --type GCP \
            --disable-custom-sans --gcp-project internal

      Create a GCP provisioner that can be used across all projects within an
      organization:

          $ step ca provisioner add Google --type GCP --gcp-organization 123456789

      Create an AWS provisioner that will only accept the SANs provided in the
      identity document and will allow multiple certificates from the same
      instance:

          $ step ca provisioner add Amazon --type AWS \
            --aws-account 123456789 --disable-custom-sans --disable-trust-on-first-use

      Create an AWS provisioner that will use a custom certificate to validate
      the instance identity documents:

          $ step ca provisioner add Amazon --type AWS \
            --aws-account 123456789
